  =, 
  'mc_2__|-'( 
     [ [  [ _A, x|...], -->, _R], 
       _T1], 
     [ [  [ _C, x|...], -->, _R], 
       _T2], 
     A), 
  [ [ assign, 
      B, 
       [ _C, -->|...]], 
    [ assign, 
      C, 
      [ call('Truth_Abduction'), '$VAR'('_T1'), '$VAR'('_T2')]], 
    [ assign, '$VAR'(0), list( [ '$VAR'(...)|...])]]].

'mc_2__|-'([[[_A, x, _B], -->, _R], _T1], [[[_C, x, _B], -->, _R], _T2], A) :-
    B=[_C, -->, _A],
    mc_2__Truth_Abduction(_T1, _T2, C),
    A=[B, C].

 (= (|- ((($A x $B) --> $R) $T1) ((($A x $C) --> $R) $T2))  
    
  ($C --> $B)

  =, 
  'mc_2__|-'( 
     [ [ _R, 
         -->, 
          [ _A, x|...]], 
       _T1], 
     [ [ _R, 
         -->, 
          [ _C, x|...]], 
       _T2], 
     A), 
  [ [ assign, 
      B, 
       [ _C, -->|...]], 
    [ assign, 
      C, 
      [ call('Truth_Induction'), '$VAR'('_T1'), '$VAR'('_T2')]], 
    [ assign, '$VAR'(0), list( [ '$VAR'(...)|...])]]].

'mc_2__|-'([[_R, -->, [_A, x, _B]], _T1], [[_R, -->, [_C, x, _B]], _T2], A) :-
    B=[_C, -->, _A],
    mc_2__Truth_Induction(_T1, _T2, C),
    A=[B, C].

'mc_2__|-'([[_R, -->, [_A, x, _B]], _T1], [[_A, -->, _C], _T2], A) :-

[ 
  =, 
  'mc_2__|-'( 
     [ [ _R, 
         -->, 
          [ _A, x|...]], 
       _T1], 
     [  [ _C, -->|...], 
       _T2], 
     A), 
  [ [ assign, 
      B, 
      [ _R, 
        -->, 
         [ _A, x|...]]], 
    [ assign, 
      C, 
      [ call('Truth_Abduction'), '$VAR'('_T1'), '$VAR'('_T2')]], 
    [ assign, '$VAR'(0), list( [ '$VAR'(...)|...])]]].

'mc_2__|-'([[_R, -->, [_A, x, _B]], _T1], [[_C, -->, _B], _T2], A) :-
    B=[_R, -->, [_A, x, _C]],
    mc_2__Truth_Abduction(_T1, _T2, C),
    A=[B, C].

;;;Whether evidence was just counted once
 (= (StampDisjoint $Ev1 $Ev2)  
  (== () 
    (collapse (let* (($x (superpose $Ev1)) ($y (superpose $Ev2))) (case (== $x $y) ((True overlap)))))))
[ 
  =, 
  mc_2__StampDisjoint(_Ev1, _Ev2, A), 
  [  [ assign, B|...], 
    [ assign, 
      C, 
      [ call(collapse), 
        [ is_p1, 
          [ [ assign, 
              _x, 
              [ call(superpose), 
                _Ev1]], 
            [ assign, 
              _y, 
              [ call(superpose), 
                _Ev2]], 
            [ assign, 
              D, 
              [ call(==), '$VAR'('_x'), '$VAR'('_y')]], 
             [ assign, E|...],

mc_3__Derive(_beliefs, _depth, _maxdepth, A) :-
    'mc_2__>'(_depth, _maxdepth, B),
    mc_3__If(B,
             is_p1(true, _beliefs),
             is_p1((mc_1__collapse(is_p1((mc_1__superpose(_beliefs, C), ['Sentence', _x, _Ev1]=C, mc_1__superpose(_beliefs, D), ['Sentence', _y, _Ev2]=D, mc_2__TupleConcat(_Ev1, _Ev2, _stamp), mc_2__StampDisjoint(_Ev1, _Ev2, E), mc_2__If(E, is_p1(('mc_2__|-'(_x, _y, F), G=[_T, _TV], (F=G*->H=[_T, _TV], mc_2__Sentence(H, _stamp, I), J=I;K='Empty', J=K)), J), L), as_p1(L, M)), M), _derivations), mc_2__TupleConcat(_beliefs, _derivations, N), 'mc_2__+'(_depth, 1, O), mc_3__Derive(N, O, _maxdepth, P)),
                   P),
             Q),
    as_p1(Q, A).

mc_3__BestCandidate(_EvaluateCandidateFunction, _BestCandidate, _tuple, A) :-
    B=[],

             is_p1(true, _BestCandidate),

                   J),
             K),
    as_p1(K, A).
